## Corpus Check
- 2484 files · ~2,564,492 words
- Verdict: corpus is large enough that graph structure adds value.

## Summary
- 30621 nodes · 34160 edges · 2679 communities (1954 shown, 725 thin omitted)
- Extraction: 96% EXTRACTED · 4% INFERRED · 0% AMBIGUOUS · INFERRED: 1340 edges (avg confidence: 0.56)
- Token cost: 0 input · 0 output

## Graph Freshness
- Built from commit: `fb8c9e66`
- Run `git rev-parse HEAD` and compare to check if the graph is stale.
- Run `graphify update .` after code changes (no API cost).

- graphify.md
- Complex filtering with Qdrant
- Each chunk has header metadata for context
- Embed the contextualized version
- Good: Filter then search
- Hybrid search with fusion
- MEMORY TYPE ARCHITECTURE (CoALA Framework):
- VECTOR STORE SELECTION:
- Query with filter
- Splits based on semantic similarity
- Then agent executes
- REACT PATTERN:
- Best for: Dynamic tasks, learning as you go
- Define minimal permissions per task type
- Review plan, then continue
- "I don't know" is a valid response
- If agent retries, external system handles duplicate
- Double context = 4x cost
- DURABLE EXECUTION:
- Execute with step limit
- Or use specialized evaluators
- See agent-memory-systems skill
- If server dies, resume later:
- Human reviews state
- Prefer fewer, more capable steps over many small ones
- Invoke with thread for state persistence
- PLAN-EXECUTE PATTERN:

- `TripRequestsPanel()` --indirect_call--> `first()`  [INFERRED]
